#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x1CD3 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x4EB3)
  1: 0x1CD6 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Restore default settings
  2: 0x1CD8 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x46AD)
  3: 0x1CDB [0x21] END_EVENT
  4: 0x1CDC [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_46AD:
  5: 0x46AD [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdi1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
```
